owners (for properties built before 1994) to install water-conserving plumbing fixtures by 2017 for single-family properties and 2019 for other properties ). Additionally, if a property is altered or improved after 2014, then water-conserving plumbing fixtures must be installed as a condition of final permit approval.&nbsp; (Cal. Civ. Code section 1101.4) \n</p><p></p>\n                            </div>\n                        </a>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n        \n\n                \n                \n\n<div class=\"col-md-7 col-xl-8 col-md-left col-block\">\n    <div class=\"featuredContentStack transactionFeatured\">\n        <div class=\"featuredInner\">\n            <div class=\"sectionBlockTitle horizontal col-xl-8\">\n                <span>Political Advocacy</span>\n            </div>\n            <div class=\"row flexRow noMarginRight\">\n                <div class=\"colLeft col-xl-8\">\n                    <div class=\"stackImage\">\n                        <img src=\"/system/homepagebucket/industry/featured/1027851/sac-cap.jpg\" alt=\"Govfeatured\">\n                    </div>\n\n\n            \n\n                \n\n            \n\n                \n\n            \n\n                \n\n            \n\n                \n\n            \n\n                \n\n            \n                    <div class=\"stackItem backgroundIndustryyellow\">\n                        <a href=\"http://www.car.org/difference/getinvolved/legislativeday/\">\n                            <div class=\"padding\">\n                                <h6 class=\"white\">C.A.R.
